in\n          <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_United_States" title="History of the United States">\n           U.S history\n          </a>\n          )\n         </small>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row" style="padding:0px 2px;white-space:nowrap">\n         Areas affected\n        </th>\n        <td style="padding:0px 2px">\n         <a href="/wiki/Hispaniola" title="Hispaniola">\n          Hispaniola\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Jamaica" title="Jamaica">\n          Jamaica\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Cuba" href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">\n          Honduras\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Belize" title="Belize">\n          Belize\n         </a>\n         , Southeast Mexico,\n         <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">\n          East Coast of the United States\n         </a>\n         (mainly in\n         <a href="/wiki/South_Florida" title="South Florida">\n          South Florida\n         </a>\n         ),\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bahamas" title="Bahamas">\n          Bahamas\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Canada" title="Atlantic Canada">\n          Atlantic Canada\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/New_Brunswick" title="New Brunswick">\n          New Brunswick\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;padding:0px 2px">\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center; border-top:#aaa 1px solid;">\n         Part of the\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">\n           2005 Atlantic hurricane season\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr style="display:none">\n        <td colspan="2">\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;padding:0px 2px">\n         <p>\n          <span class="noprint">\n           <b>\n            History\n           </b>\n          </span>\n         </p>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <span class="noprint">\n            <small>\n             <a href="/wiki/Meteorological_history_of_Hurricane_Wilma" title="Meteorological history of Hurricane Wilma">\n              Meteorological history\n             </a>\n            </small>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n         <p>\n          <span class="noprint">\n           <b>\n            Effects\n           </b>\n          </span>\n         </p>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <span class="noprint">\n            <small>\n             <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Wilma_in_Florida" title="Effects of Hurricane Wilma in Florida">\n              Florida\n             </a>\n            </small>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <span class="noprint">\n            <small>\n             <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Wilma_in_The_Bahamas" title="Effects of Hurricane Wilma in The Bahamas">\n              The Bahamas\n             </a>\n            </small>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n         <p>\n          <span class="noprint">\n           <b>\n            Other wikis\n           </b>\n          </span>\n         </p>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <span class="noprint">\n            <small>\n             <a class="extiw" href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:Hurricane_Wilma" title="commons:Category:Hurricane Wilma">\n              Commons: Wilma images\n             </a>\n            </small>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Hurricane Wilma\n       </b>\n       was the most intense\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone" title="Tropical cyclone">\n        tropical cyclone\n       </a>\n       ever recorded in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">\n        Atlantic basin\n       </a>\n       , as well as the most intense recorded in the western hemisphere until\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Patricia" title="Hurricane Patricia">\n        Hurricane Patricia\n       </a>\n       in 2015. Part of the record-breaking\n       <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2005 Atlantic hurricane season\n       </a>\n       , which included three of the top ten\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_the_most_intense_tropical_cyclones#North_Atlantic_Ocean" title="List of the most intense tropical cyclones">\n        most intense Atlantic hurricanes\n       </a>\n       ever (along with #4\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Rita" title="Hurricane Rita">\n        Rita\n       </a>\n       and #7\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katrina" title="Hurricane Katrina">\n        Katrina\n       </a>\n       ), Wilma was the twenty-second storm, thirteenth\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone" title="Tropical cyclone">\n        hurricane\n       </a>\n       , sixth\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Major_hurricane" title="Major hurricane">\n        major hurricane\n       </a>\n       , fourth\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saffir-Simpson_Hurricane_Scale" title="Saffir-Simpson Hurricane Scale">\n        Category 5\n       </a>\n       hurricane, and second-most destructive hurricane of the 2005\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="Atlantic hurricane season">\n        season\n       </a>\n       . A\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_depression" title="Tropical depression">\n        tropical depression\n       </a>\n       formed in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Sea" title="Caribbean Sea">\n        Caribbean Sea\n       </a>\n       near\n       <a href="/wiki/Jamaica" title="Jamaica">\n        Jamaica\n       </a>\n       on October 15, headed westward, and two days later intensified into a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_storm" title="Tropical storm">\n        tropical storm\n       </a>\n       which turned abruptly southward and was named\n       <i>\n        Wilma\n       </i>\n       . Wilma continued to strengthen, and eventually became a hurricane on October 18. Shortly thereafter, explosive intensification occurred, and in only 24 hours, Wilma became a Category 5 hurricane with wind speeds of 185 miles per hour (298\xc2\xa0km/h).\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Wilma\'s intensity slowly leveled off after becoming a Category 5 hurricane, and winds had decreased to 150 miles per hour (240\xc2\xa0km/h) before it reached the\n       <a href="/wiki/Yucat%C3%A1n_Peninsula" title="Yucat\xc3\xa1n Peninsula">\n        Yucat\xc3\xa1n Peninsula\n       </a>\n       on October 20 and 21. After crossing the Yucat\xc3\xa1n, Wilma emerged into the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">\n        Gulf of Mexico\n       </a>\n       as a Category 2 hurricane. As Wilma began accelerating to the northeast, gradual re-intensification occurred, and the hurricane was upgraded to Category 3 on October 24. Shortly thereafter, Wilma made landfall in\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Romano" title="Cape Romano">\n        Cape Romano\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">\n        Florida\n       </a>\n       with winds of 120 miles per hour (190\xc2\xa0km/h). As Wilma was crossing Florida, it briefly weakened back to a Category 2 hurricane, but again re-intensified as it reached the Atlantic Ocean. The hurricane intensified into a Category 3 hurricane for the last time but dropped below that intensity while accelerating northeastward. By October 26, Wilma transitioned into an\n       <a href="/wiki/Extratropical_cyclone" title="Extratropical cyclone">\n        extratropical cyclone\n       </a>\n       southeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Nova_Scotia" title="Nova Scotia">\n        Nova Scotia\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Wilma made several landfalls, with the most destructive effects felt in the Yucat\xc3\xa1n Peninsula of\n       <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">\n        Mexico\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">\n        Cuba\n       </a>\n       , and the U.S. state of Florida. At least 62 deaths were reported, and damage total estimated at\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USD" title="USD">\n        $\n       </a>\n       29.4\xc2\xa0billion (equivalent to $36.1\xc2\xa0billion in 2017), with in the United States $21\xc2\xa0billion ($25.8\xc2\xa0billion in 2017).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_1-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As a result, Wilma is ranked as the sixth costliest hurricane in United States history. Wilma was the most recent\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_hurricane_wind_scale#Category_3" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson hurricane wind scale">\n        major hurricane\n       </a>\n       to make landfall in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Contiguous_United_States" title="Contiguous United States">\n        contiguous United States\n       </a>\n       until\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Harvey" title="Hurricane Harvey">\n        Hurricane Harvey\n       </a>\n       made landfall in southern\n       <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">\n        Texas\n       </a>\n       on August 26, 2017, ending a record length of time \xe2\x80\x93 slightly over 11 years and 10 months \xe2\x80\x93 without any major hurricanes making landfall in the United States. Wilma was also the last hurricane to strike the state of Florida until\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hermine" title="Hurricane Hermine">\n        Hurricane Hermine\n       </a>\n       did so nearly 11 years later in 2016, another record. Wilma was also the last major hurricane to make landfall in Florida until\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irma" title="Hurricane Irma">\n        Hurricane Irma\n       </a>\n       made landfall in early September 2017.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toc" id="toc">\n       <div class="toctitle">\n        <h2>\n         Contents\n        </h2>\n       </div>\n       <ul>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1">\n         <a href="#Meteorological_history">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           1\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Meteorological history\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-2">\n         <a href="#Preparations">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           2\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Preparations\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-3">\n           <a href="#Cayman_Islands_and_Central_America">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             2.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Cayman Islands and Central America\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-4">\n           <a href="#Mexico">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             2.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Mexico\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-5">\n           <a href="#Cuba">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             2.3\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Cuba\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-6">\n           <a href="#Florida">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             2.4\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Florida\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-7">\n           <a href="#The_Bahamas">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             2.5\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             The Bahamas\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-8">\n         <a href="#Impact">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           3\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Impact\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-9">\n           <a href="#Caribbean">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Caribbean\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-10">\n           <a href="#Mexico_2">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Mexico\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-11">\n           <a href="#Cuba_2">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.3\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Cuba\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-12">\n           <a href="#United_States">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.4\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             United States\n            </span>\n           </a>\n           <ul>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-13">\n             <a href="#Florida_2">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               3.4.1\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Florida\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-14">\n             <a href="#Elsewhere_in_the_United_States">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               3.4.2\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Elsewhere in the United States\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n           </ul>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-15">\n           <a href="#Bahamas">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.5\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Bahamas\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-16">\n         <a href="#Aftermath">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           4\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Aftermath\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-17">\n           <a href="#United_States_2">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             4.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             United States\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-18">\n           <a href="#Mexico_3">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             4.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Mexico\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-19">\n           <a href="#Cuba_3">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             4.3\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Cuba\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-20">\n           <a href="#Retirement">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             4.4\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Retirement\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-21">\n         <a href="#Records_and_naming">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           5\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Records and naming\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-22">\n         <a href="#See_also">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           6\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           See also\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-23">\n         <a href="#References">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           7\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           References\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-24">\n         <a href="#External_links">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           8\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           External links\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Meteorological_history">\n        Meteorological history\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Meteorological history">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Meteorological_history_of_Hurricane_Wilma" title="Meteorological history of Hurricane Wilma">\n        Meteorological history of Hurricane Wilma\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wilma_2005_track.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="904" data-file-width="1024" height="194" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Wilma_2005_track.png/220px-Wilma_2005_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Wilma_2005_track.png/330px-Wilma_2005_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Wilma_2005_track.png/440px-Wilma_2005_track.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wilma_2005_track.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Map plotting the track and intensity of the storm, according to the\n         <a href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_scale" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale">\n          Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       A large area of disturbed weather developed across much of the Caribbean Sea during mid-October as a lower-tropospheric low interacted with a broad area of disturbed weather, aided by an upper-level low across the region. A broad\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Low_pressure_area" title="Low pressure area">\n        area of low pressure\n       </a>\n       developed on October 13 to the southeast of Jamaica, and slowly became more concentrated as upper-level\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       gradually decreased.\n       <a href="/wiki/Dvorak_technique" title="Dvorak technique">\n        Dvorak classifications\n       </a>\n       began on October 14, and by late October 15 the surface circulation in the system became well enough defined, with sufficiently organized deep convection, for the National Hurricane Center to designate the system as Tropical Depression Twenty-Four while located about 220\xc2\xa0mi (350\xc2\xa0km) east-southeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Cayman" title="Grand Cayman">\n        Grand Cayman\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_1-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The depression drifted southwestward because of the influence of two\n       <a href="/wiki/Ridge_(meteorology)" title="Ridge (meteorology)">\n        ridges\n       </a>\n       to its north and with warm\n       <a href="/wiki/Sea_surface_temperature" title="Sea surface temperature">\n        sea surface temperatures\n       </a>\n       and a favorable upper-level environment, it strengthened into Tropical Storm Wilma on October 17. Initially, development was slow, due to the large size of the storm and a flat\n       <a href="/wiki/Pressure_gradient" title="Pressure gradient">\n        pressure gradient\n       </a>\n       . However, convection gradually organized, and from October 18 through October 19, Wilma underwent\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rapid_deepening" title="Rapid deepening">\n        explosive deepening\n       </a>\n       over the open waters of the Caribbean Sea. Around 12:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa018, the system intensified into a hurricane. In a 30\xe2\x80\x91hour period, the pressure dropped from 982\n       <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n        mbar\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n        hPa\n       </a>\n       ; 29.00\n       <a href="/wiki/Inch_of_mercury" title="Inch of mercury">\n        inHg\n       </a>\n       ) to the record-low of 882\xc2\xa0mbar (hPa; 26.05\xc2\xa0inHg), while the winds increased to 185\xc2\xa0mph (295\xc2\xa0km/h). During its intensification on October\xc2\xa019, the hurricane\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">\n        eye\n       </a>\n       shrank to as small as 2.3\xc2\xa0mi (3.7\xc2\xa0km) in diameter, becoming the smallest eye ever seen in a tropical cyclone.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_1-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <div class="PopUpMediaTransform" id="mwe_player_0" style="width:220px;" videopayload=\'&lt;div class="mediaContainer" style="width:480px"&gt;&lt;video id="mwe_player_1" poster="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Hurricane_Wilma.ogv/480px--Hurricane_Wilma.ogv.jpg" controls="" preload="none" autoplay="" style="width:480px;height:320px" class="kskin" data-durationhint="13.333333333333" data-startoffset="0" data-mwtitle="Hurricane_Wilma.ogv" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons"&gt;&lt;source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/02/Hurricane_Wilma.ogv" type="video/ogg; codecs=&amp;quot;theora&amp;quot;" data-title="Original Ogg file, 480 \xc3\x97 320 (1.59 Mbps)" data-shorttitle="Ogg source" data-width="480" data-height="320" data-bandwidth="1588671" data-framerate="30"/&gt;&lt;source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/0/02/Hurricane_Wilma.ogv/Hurricane_Wilma.ogv.160p.webm" type="video/webm; codecs=&amp;quot;vp8, vorbis&amp;quot;" data-title="Low bandwidth WebM (160P)" data-shorttitle="WebM 160P" data-transcodekey="160p.webm" data-width="240" data-height="160" data-bandwidth="129888" data-framerate="30"/&gt;&lt;source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/0/02/Hurricane_Wilma.ogv/Hurricane_Wilma.ogv.240p.webm" type="video/webm; codecs=&amp;quot;vp8, vorbis&amp;quot;" data-title="Small WebM (240P)" data-shorttitle="WebM 240P" data-transcodekey="240p.webm" data-width="360" data-height="240" data-bandwidth="260848" data-framerate="30"/&gt;&lt;/video&gt;&lt;/div&gt;\'>\n         <img alt="File:Hurricane Wilma.ogv" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Hurricane_Wilma.ogv/220px--Hurricane_Wilma.ogv.jpg" style="width:220px;height:147px"/>\n         <a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/02/Hurricane_Wilma.ogv" target="new" title="Play media">\n          <span class="play-btn-large">\n           <span class="mw-tmh-playtext">\n            Play media\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Wilma.ogv" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Satellite video of Wilma\'s lifespan.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On October\xc2\xa020, Wilma weakened below Category 5 intensity to 155\xc2\xa0mph (250\xc2\xa0km/h) due to an\n       <a href="/wiki/Eyewall_replacement_cycle" title="Eyewall replacement cycle">\n        eyewall replacement cycle\n       </a>\n       , began to turn towards the northwest, and further slowed its movement. Late on October\xc2\xa021, Wilma made landfall on the island of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cozumel" title="Cozumel">\n        Cozumel\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Quintana_Roo" title="Quintana Roo">\n        Quintana Roo\n       </a>\n       , at around 21:45\xc2\xa0UTC with maximum sustained winds of 150\xc2\xa0mph (240\xc2\xa0km/h) and then again made a second landfall on the Mexican mainland six hours later and only slightly weaker. Wilma continued to slowly drift towards the north over the Yucat\xc3\xa1n Peninsula, although it weakened to a moderate hurricane while over land, it reemerged over the southern Gulf of Mexico on October 23 around 00:00\xc2\xa0UTC. Despite Wilma spending 24 hours over land, it re\xc3\xabmerged with little intensity lost, and began to re-intensify shortly after. This was perhaps due to its large size and because the majority of its circulation remained over the warm waters of the northwest Caribbean and Gulf of Mexico. A powerful\n       <a href="/wiki/Trough_(meteorology)" title="Trough (meteorology)">\n        trough\n       </a>\n       turned the hurricane to the northeast and accelerated its forward motion. Its large eye remained well-organized, and Wilma intensified, despite increasing amounts of wind shear, briefly producing winds of 125\xc2\xa0mph (200\xc2\xa0km/h), before making landfall on\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Romano" title="Cape Romano">\n        Cape Romano\n       </a>\n       , Florida, as a 120\xc2\xa0mph (195\xc2\xa0km/h) major hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_1-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Wilma crossed the state in about 4.6\xc2\xa0hours and weakened to a Category 2 hurricane, with winds of 110\xc2\xa0mph (175\xc2\xa0km/h), after entering the Atlantic Ocean near\n       <a href="/wiki/Jupiter,_Florida" title="Jupiter, Florida">\n        Jupiter, Florida\n       </a>\n       . Key West received several feet of water in the low-lying areas and flooded homes. The Lower Keys also experienced an unusual flood: it occurred twice. First, as the storm approached Florida, it pushed water across the keys from south to north. As the storm finally crossed into the Everglades, all the water that had been pushed by the storm was released as Wilma crossed the peninsula. The water then raced back across the Lower Keys a second time and went back out to sea. This caused additional flooding and costly damage. Possibly due to less friction of the eyewall or moving over warm waters of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulf_Stream" title="Gulf Stream">\n        Gulf Stream\n       </a>\n       , Wilma again re-intensified to reach winds of 125\xc2\xa0mph (200\xc2\xa0km/h) and subsequently absorbed\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Alpha" title="Tropical Storm Alpha">\n        Tropical Storm Alpha\n       </a>\n       to the south, before cold air and wind shear penetrated the inner core of convection. On October 26, Wilma transitioned into an\n       <a href="/wiki/Extratropical_cyclone" title="Extratropical cyclone">\n        extratropical cyclone\n       </a>\n       , and on the next day, the remnants of Wilma were absorbed by another extratropical storm over\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Canada" title="Atlantic Canada">\n        Atlantic Canada\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_1-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Preparations">\n        Preparations\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Preparations">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Cayman_Islands_and_Central_America">\n        Cayman Islands and Central America\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Cayman Islands and Central America">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       (NHC) issued many\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_warnings_and_watches" title="Tropical cyclone warnings and watches">\n        tropical cyclone warnings and watches\n       </a>\n       throughout Wilma\'s duration. At 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa016, a hurricane watch and tropical storm warning were posted for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands" title="Cayman Islands">\n        Cayman Islands\n       </a>\n       . A tropical storm warning was issued in\n       <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">\n        Honduras\n       </a>\n       from the border with\n       <a href="/wiki/Nicaragua" title="Nicaragua">\n        Nicaragua\n       </a>\n       westward to Cabo Camaron at 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa017. The hurricane watch and tropical storm warning for the Cayman Islands were both discontinued at 18:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa019. In\n       <a href="/wiki/Belize" title="Belize">\n        Belize\n       </a>\n       , another tropical storm warning became in effect at 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa019 from the border with Mexico to\n       <a href="/wiki/Belize_City" title="Belize City">\n        Belize City\n       </a>\n       . On October\xc2\xa021, the tropical storm warning in Honduras was discontinued at 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC, while the other in Belize was canceled twelve hours later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_1-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mexico">\n        Mexico\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Mexico">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Wilma_21_oct_2005_1625Z.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="8400" data-file-width="6400" height="289" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/Hurricane_Wilma_21_oct_2005_1625Z.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Wilma_21_oct_2005_1625Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/Hurricane_Wilma_21_oct_2005_1625Z.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Wilma_21_oct_2005_1625Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/Hurricane_Wilma_21_oct_2005_1625Z.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Wilma_21_oct_2005_1625Z.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Wilma_21_oct_2005_1625Z.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Hurricane Wilma about to cross\n         <a href="/wiki/Cozumel" title="Cozumel">\n          Cozumel\n         </a>\n         , a small island just off the Yucat\xc3\xa1n Peninsula coast. Winds are at 150\xc2\xa0mph (240\xc2\xa0km/h) as the eyewall passes over the island, and hurricane-strength winds extended for 80\xc2\xa0mi (130\xc2\xa0km) from the storm\xe2\x80\x99s center.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Quintana_Roo" title="Quintana Roo">\n        Quintana Roo\n       </a>\n       government officials declared a red alert on the evening of Wednesday, October 19. Classes were suspended in the state\'s northern\n       <a href="/wiki/Municipalities_of_Quintana_Roo" title="Municipalities of Quintana Roo">\n        municipalities\n       </a>\n       and residents of coastal areas were advised to take refuge farther inland; tourists in the resort city of\n       <a href="/wiki/Canc%C3%BAn" title="Canc\xc3\xban">\n        Canc\xc3\xban\n       </a>\n       and its adjacent islands were told to return to their places of origin or head inland while those unable to were relocated to designated hurricane shelters throughout the city. In neighboring\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yucat%C3%A1n_(state)" title="Yucat\xc3\xa1n (state)">\n        Yucat\xc3\xa1n\n       </a>\n       , classes were also suspended in 18 coastal\n       <a href="/wiki/Municipalities_of_Yucat%C3%A1n" title="Municipalities of Yucat\xc3\xa1n">\n        municipalities\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-universal_2-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-universal-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Cuba">\n        Cuba\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Cuba">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">\n        Cuba\n       </a>\n       , a hurricane watch was issued from\n       <a href="/wiki/Matanzas_Province" title="Matanzas Province">\n        Matanzas Province\n       </a>\n       westward to\n       <a href="/wiki/Pinar_del_R%C3%ADo_Province" title="Pinar del R\xc3\xado Province">\n        Pinar del R\xc3\xado Province\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Isla_de_la_Juventud" title="Isla de la Juventud">\n        Isla de la Juventud\n       </a>\n       at 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa018. Early on October\xc2\xa020, a tropical storm warning was posted for\n       <a href="/wiki/La_Habana_Province" title="La Habana Province">\n        La Habana\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Havana" title="Havana">\n        Ciudad de La Habana\n       </a>\n       , and Pinar del R\xc3\xado provinces. The hurricane watch was upgraded to a hurricane warning for Ciudad de la Habana, La Habana, and Pinar del Rio provinces at 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa022. All warnings and watches for Cuba were discontinued late on October\xc2\xa024.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_1-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Preparations were made to evacuate four western\n       <a href="/wiki/Provinces_of_Cuba" title="Provinces of Cuba">\n        provinces\n       </a>\n       , including the\n       <a href="/wiki/Isla_de_la_Juventud" title="Isla de la Juventud">\n        Isle of Youth\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bbc-1_3-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bbc-1-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In all, over 760,000\xc2\xa0people were ordered to evacuate.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReliefWeb-2006-24_4-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ReliefWeb-2006-24-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Florida">\n        Florida\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Florida">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Wilma_in_Florida" title="Effects of Hurricane Wilma in Florida">\n        Effects of Hurricane Wilma in Florida\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wilma05FLLandfallRadar.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="455" data-file-width="598" height="167" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Wilma05FLLandfallRadar.png/220px-Wilma05FLLandfallRadar.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Wilma05FLLandfallRadar.png/330px-Wilma05FLLandfallRadar.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Wilma05FLLandfallRadar.png/440px-Wilma05FLLandfallRadar.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wilma05FLLandfallRadar.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Radar image of Hurricane Wilma making landfall in\n         <a href="/wiki/South_Florida" title="South Florida">\n          South Florida\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center (NHC)\n       </a>\n       issued many tropical cyclone warnings and watches in Florida, beginning with a hurricane watch in\n       <a href="/wiki/Florida_Keys" title="Florida Keys">\n        Florida Keys\n       </a>\n       including\n       <a href="/wiki/Dry_Tortugas" title="Dry Tortugas">\n        Dry Tortugas\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Florida_Bay" title="Florida Bay">\n        Florida Bay\n       </a>\n       at 15:00\n       <a href="/wiki/Coordinated_Universal_Time" title="Coordinated Universal Time">\n        UTC\n       </a>\n       on October\xc2\xa022. Six hours later, the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center (NHC)\n       </a>\n       issued another hurricane watch for the west coast of Florida south of\n       <a href="/wiki/Longboat_Key,_Florida" title="Longboat Key, Florida">\n        Longboat Key\n       </a>\n       and on the east coast of Florida to the south of\n       <a href="/wiki/Titusville,_Florida" title="Titusville, Florida">\n        Titusville\n       </a>\n       , including\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Okeechobee" title="Lake Okeechobee">\n        Lake Okeechobee\n       </a>\n       . At 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa023, a tropical storm watch was put into effect on the west coast from Longboat Key northward to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Steinhatchee_River" title="Steinhatchee River">\n        Steinhatchee River\n       </a>\n       and on the east coast from Titusville northward to\n       <a href="/wiki/Fernandina_Beach,_Florida" title="Fernandina Beach, Florida">\n        Fernandina Beach\n       </a>\n       . Early the following day, the hurricane watch was upgraded to a hurricane warning on the west coast and on the east coast from\n       <a href="/wiki/Jupiter_Inlet_Light" title="Jupiter Inlet Light">\n        Jupiter Inlet\n       </a>\n       southward, including Lake Okeechobee.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_1-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The hurricane warning along the east coast stretching from the Jupiter Inlet southward was expended northward to Titusville at 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa023. Simultaneously, the portion of the tropical storm watch from Titusville to\n       <a href="/wiki/Flagler_Beach,_Florida" title="Flagler Beach, Florida">\n        Flagler Beach\n       </a>\n       was upgraded to a tropical storm warning. The tropical storm warning was extended further northward to\n       <a href="/wiki/St._Augustine,_Florida" title="St. Augustine, Florida">\n        St. Augustine\n       </a>\n       at 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa024. Twelve hours later, the tropical storm watch was discontinued from St. Augustine to Fernandina Beach. At 17:00\xc2\xa0UTC, the tropical storm warning from Longboat Key to the Steinhatchee River was canceled. The remainder of the hurricane warning in effect was downgraded to a tropical storm warning about 90\xc2\xa0minutes later. By 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa024, all remaining tropical cyclone warnings and watches were discontinued.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_1-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       A mandatory evacuation of residents was ordered for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Florida_Keys" title="Florida Keys">\n        Florida Keys\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Monroe_County,_Florida" title="Monroe County, Florida">\n        Monroe County\n       </a>\n       and those in Collier County living west or south of\n       <a href="/wiki/U.S._Route_41_in_Florida" title="U.S. Route 41 in Florida">\n        US 41\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-collier-evac_5-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-collier-evac-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       County offices, schools and courts were closed Monday, October 24. At least 300 Keys evacuees were housed at the Monroe County shelter at\n       <a href="/wiki/Florida_International_University" title="Florida International University">\n        Florida International University\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Miami-Dade_County,_Florida" title="Miami-Dade County, Florida">\n        Miami-Dade County\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-monroecounty_6-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-monroecounty-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       All\n       <a href="/wiki/Collier_County,_Florida" title="Collier County, Florida">\n        Collier County\n       </a>\n       public schools were declared closed for Friday, October 21. The schools were closed to "allow parents and staff to prepare for the storm and potential evacuation", and also allowed "for needed preparation of schools to be used as hurricane shelters." The schools remained closed on Monday, October 24, as the hurricane made landfall.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-collier_7-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-collier-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Schools around\n       <a href="/wiki/Fort_Myers,_Florida" title="Fort Myers, Florida">\n        Fort Myers\n       </a>\n       and Tampa, as well as\n       <a href="/wiki/Sumter_County,_Florida" title="Sumter County, Florida">\n        Sumter\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Marion_County,_Florida" title="Marion County, Florida">\n        Marion\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Osceola_County,_Florida" title="Osceola County, Florida">\n        Osceola\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Pasco_County,_Florida" title="Pasco County, Florida">\n        Pasco\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Polk_County,_Florida" title="Polk County, Florida">\n        Polk\n       </a>\n       counties, were closed on Monday, October 24. In other areas of Central Florida, schools were closed in\n       <a href="/wiki/Flagler_County,_Florida" title="Flagler County, Florida">\n        Flagler\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_County,_Florida" title="Lake County, Florida">\n        Lake\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Orange_County,_Florida" title="Orange County, Florida">\n        Orange\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Volusia_County,_Florida" title="Volusia County, Florida">\n        Volusia\n       </a>\n       counties.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-schoolclosed_8-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-schoolclosed-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Schools in\n       <a href="/wiki/Palm_Beach_County,_Florida" title="Palm Beach County, Florida">\n        Palm Beach\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Broward_County,_Florida" title="Broward County, Florida">\n        Broward\n       </a>\n       counties were closed for two weeks because of extended power outages and some damage to school buildings.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Schools in\n       <a href="/wiki/Collier_County,_Florida" title="Collier County, Florida">\n        Collier\n       </a>\n       and Miami-Dade counties were closed for a little over a week, including the\n       <a href="/wiki/University_of_Miami" title="University of Miami">\n        University of Miami\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Orange_juice" title="Orange juice">\n        Orange juice\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Futures_contract" title="Futures contract">\n        futures\n       </a>\n       reached the highest level in six years on Wednesday, October 19, 2005, closing up 2.9 cents at US$1.118 per pound.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-accuweather_10-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-accuweather-10">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As dynamic models moved the storm\'s track east over Florida,\n       <a href="/wiki/Petroleum" title="Petroleum">\n        oil\n       </a>\n       futures eased as worries of another direct hit on the oil-producing regions of the Gulf of Mexico subsided.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       College and professional hockey games scheduled the weekend before Wilma\'s landfall were rescheduled for a later time. The professional football game scheduled for Sunday was moved ahead to Friday night. A concert by the industrial rock band\n       <a href="/wiki/Nine_Inch_Nails" title="Nine Inch Nails">\n        Nine Inch Nails\n       </a>\n       , expected to have taken place Monday, October 24, was postponed and later cancelled. Key West\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Fantasy_Fest" title="Fantasy Fest">\n        Fantasy Fest\n       </a>\n       held around each\n       <a href="/wiki/Halloween" title="Halloween">\n        Halloween\n       </a>\n       was postponed until December.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="The_Bahamas">\n        The Bahamas\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: The Bahamas">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       At 12:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa023, about 24\xc2\xa0hours before Wilma made its closest approach to the archipelago, the government of The Bahamas issued a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_warnings_and_watches" title="Tropical cyclone warnings and watches">\n        hurricane warning\n       </a>\n       for the northwestern portion of the territory, including the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Abacos" title="Abacos">\n        Abacos\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Andros,_Bahamas" title="Andros, Bahamas">\n        Andros Island\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Berry_Islands" title="Berry Islands">\n        Berry Islands\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Bimini" title="Bimini">\n        Bimini\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Eleuthera" title="Eleuthera">\n        Eleuthera\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Bahama" title="Grand Bahama">\n        Grand Bahama\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Providence" title="New Providence">\n        New Providence\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_1-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The government of The Bahamas advised citizens to rush preparations to completion, though many failed to fully prepare, believing Wilma would pass through the region as a tropical storm. Many homes failed to board windows or apply hurricane shutters, as well. Officials ordered evacuations for the eastern and western portion of Grand Bahama island, and established multiple shelters on the island.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bvg_13-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bvg-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Evacuations were minimal; it is estimated that between 300 and 1,000 people left.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bvg_13-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bvg-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ifrc1_14-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ifrc1-14">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As most people failed to prepare sufficiently for the hurricane, hardware stores and food markets were generally well-stocked.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bvg_13-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bvg-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:right; float:right;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Impact">\n        Impact\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Impact">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <table class="wikitable sortable" style="float:right">\n       <caption>\n        Impact by country\n       </caption>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         Region\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Deaths\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Damage (USD)\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         The Bahamas\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7008100000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $100\xc2\xa0million\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Cuba\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         4\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7008700000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $700\xc2\xa0million\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Haiti\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         12\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7005500000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $500\xc2\xa0thousand\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Jamaica\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7007935000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $93.5\xc2\xa0million\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Mexico\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         8\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7009750000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $7.5\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         United States\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         62\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7010210070000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $21\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr class="sortbottom">\n        <th>\n         Total\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         87\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         $29.394\xc2\xa0billion\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Wilma was responsible for 87 total deaths and almost $29.4\xc2\xa0billion (2005 US$) in damages.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Caribbean">\n        Caribbean\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Caribbean">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">\n        Haiti\n       </a>\n       , the outer bands of Wilma triggered\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mudslide" title="Mudslide">\n        mudslides\n       </a>\n       , killing at least 12\xc2\xa0people.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-yahoonews-1_15-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-yahoonews-1-15">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Damage in the country totaled around $500,000 (2005\xc2\xa0USD).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-emdat_16-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-emdat-16">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Wilma caused one death in Jamaica as a tropical depression on October 16. It pounded the island for three days ending on October 18, flooding several low-lying communities and triggering mudslides that blocked roads and damaged several homes. Almost 250\xc2\xa0people were in emergency shelters on the island.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ndtv-1_17-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ndtv-1-17">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Damage on the island totaled $93.5\xc2\xa0million (2005\xc2\xa0USD).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">\n        <a href="#cite_note-18">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mexico_2">\n        Mexico\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Mexico">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wilma_in_cozumel_island-109920_m.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="482" data-file-width="642" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Wilma_in_cozumel_island-109920_m.jpg/220px-Wilma_in_cozumel_island-109920_m.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Wilma_in_cozumel_island-109920_m.jpg/330px-Wilma_in_cozumel_island-109920_m.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Wilma_in_cozumel_island-109920_m.jpg/440px-Wilma_in_cozumel_island-109920_m.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wilma_in_cozumel_island-109920_m.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The island of Cozumel is shown through the eye of Hurricane Wilma in this composite image. NOAA\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       At least eight deaths were reported in Mexico. Five were in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Playa_del_Carmen" title="Playa del Carmen">\n        Playa del Carmen\n       </a>\n       area due to a gas explosion caused by the strong winds. Four deaths also were reported in\n       <a href="/wiki/Cozumel" title="Cozumel">\n        Cozumel\n       </a>\n       and another in\n       <a href="/wiki/Canc%C3%BAn" title="Canc\xc3\xban">\n        Canc\xc3\xban\n       </a>\n       due to wind blowing a window out. Another death, caused by a falling tree, was reported in the state of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yucat%C3%A1n_(state)" title="Yucat\xc3\xa1n (state)">\n        Yucat\xc3\xa1n\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ap-0919-23_19-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ap-0919-23-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Pictures and television reports indicated extensive structural damage throughout the\n       <a href="/wiki/Canc%C3%BAn" title="Canc\xc3\xban">\n        Canc\xc3\xban\n       </a>\n       area, as well as significant\n       <a href="/wiki/Flood" title="Flood">\n        flooding\n       </a>\n       and many downed trees,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Power_line" title="Power line">\n        power lines\n       </a>\n       and scattered debris. Several homes had also collapsed. Rainfall amounts in excess of 23\xc2\xa0inches (590\xc2\xa0mm) were reported in several areas, with\n       <a href="/wiki/Isla_Mujeres" title="Isla Mujeres">\n        Isla Mujeres\n       </a>\n       reporting 64\xc2\xa0inches (1,625.6\xc2\xa0mm)\xe2\x80\x94five times what\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Gilbert" title="Hurricane Gilbert">\n        Hurricane Gilbert\n       </a>\n       dropped.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">\n        <a href="#cite_note-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The station recorded 64.33\xc2\xa0inches (1,633.98\xc2\xa0mm) over 24\xc2\xa0hours, setting a western hemisphere record for the greatest rainfall in that time period.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">\n        <a href="#cite_note-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One gymnasium used as a shelter lost its roof, which forced the evacuation of more than 1,000\xc2\xa0people staying there.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ap-0919-23_19-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ap-0919-23-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During the storm, waves five to eight meters high (enough to reach the third floor of many hotels) slammed against the coastline.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Eluniversal_22-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Eluniversal-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Damage was extensive as well on Cozumel, with many broken windows, fallen trees and power lines, but less structural damage. It was comparable to the scene after\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Emily_(2005)" title="Hurricane Emily (2005)">\n        Hurricane Emily\n       </a>\n       back in July 2005, a storm of similar intensity at landfall, but faster moving.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The governor of\n       <a href="/wiki/Quintana_Roo" title="Quintana Roo">\n        Quintana Roo\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9lix_Gonz%C3%A1lez_Canto" title="F\xc3\xa9lix Gonz\xc3\xa1lez Canto">\n        F\xc3\xa9lix Gonz\xc3\xa1lez Canto\n       </a>\n       , said in an interview: "Never in the history of Quintana Roo have we seen a storm like this."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ap-0025-23_23-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ap-0025-23-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Communication was initially limited, as telephone and electric services were completely out in the affected areas; however, in downtown\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canc%C3%BAn,_Mexico" title="Canc\xc3\xban, Mexico">\n        Canc\xc3\xban\n       </a>\n       , some telephone communications remained intact, and tourists went out and risked their lives to contact home. There were also extensive reports of\n       <a href="/wiki/Looting" title="Looting">\n        looting\n       </a>\n       of many businesses in\n       <a href="/wiki/Quintana_Roo" title="Quintana Roo">\n        Quintana Roo\n       </a>\n       , particularly in Canc\xc3\xban.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ap-0919-23_19-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ap-0919-23-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Canc%C3%BAn,_Hurac%C3%A1n_Wilma,_Oct_22.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Canc%C3%BAn%2C_Hurac%C3%A1n_Wilma%2C_Oct_22.jpg/220px-Canc%C3%BAn%2C_Hurac%C3%A1n_Wilma%2C_Oct_22.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Canc%C3%BAn%2C_Hurac%C3%A1n_Wilma%2C_Oct_22.jpg/330px-Canc%C3%BAn%2C_Hurac%C3%A1n_Wilma%2C_Oct_22.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Canc%C3%BAn%2C_Hurac%C3%A1n_Wilma%2C_Oct_22.jpg/440px-Canc%C3%BAn%2C_Hurac%C3%A1n_Wilma%2C_Oct_22.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Canc%C3%BAn,_Hurac%C3%A1n_Wilma,_Oct_22.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Damage to a McDonald\'s in\n         <a href="/wiki/Canc%C3%BAn" title="Canc\xc3\xban">\n          Canc\xc3\xban\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       After Wilma passed, a sense of desperation developed in the region because people were being held in shelters due to the extensive damage. Thousands of tourists remained stranded in shelters, and the priority was to send them home immediately, according to\n       <a href="/wiki/President_of_Mexico" title="President of Mexico">\n        President\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Vicente_Fox" title="Vicente Fox">\n        Vicente Fox\n       </a>\n       . Buses arrived in Canc\xc3\xban from\n       <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A9rida,_Yucat%C3%A1n" title="M\xc3\xa9rida, Yucat\xc3\xa1n">\n        M\xc3\xa9rida\n       </a>\n       , where tourists were hoping to find flights home. The United States\n       <a href="/wiki/Diplomatic_mission" title="Diplomatic mission">\n        embassy\n       </a>\n       told tourists to go to M\xc3\xa9rida, although the next day they had to change their announcements because M\xc3\xa9rida had become so packed with people. The road to M\xc3\xa9rida was very dangerous and practically impassable for taxis, yet people dealt with the exorbitant fees being charged for passage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24">\n        <a href="#cite_note-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The destruction left behind by Wilma in the Yucat\xc3\xa1n severely damaged the tourist industry there, as the storm affected some of the tourist hot spots of Mexico. Damage in Mexico totaled $7.5\xc2\xa0billion (2005\xc2\xa0USD, $80\xc2\xa0billion 2005 MXN), of which $4.6\xc2\xa0billion (2005\xc2\xa0USD, $50\xc2\xa0billion 2005 MXN) was from agricultural damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ciclones_25-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ciclones-25">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Cuba_2">\n        Cuba\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Cuba">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Wilma_23_oct_2005_1615Z.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="7200" data-file-width="6400" height="248" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Hurricane_Wilma_23_oct_2005_1615Z.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Wilma_23_oct_2005_1615Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Hurricane_Wilma_23_oct_2005_1615Z.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Wilma_23_oct_2005_1615Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Hurricane_Wilma_23_oct_2005_1615Z.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Wilma_23_oct_2005_1615Z.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Wilma_23_oct_2005_1615Z.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Hurricane Wilma west of Cuba on October\xc2\xa023\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">\n        Cuba\n       </a>\n       , a\n       <a href="/wiki/Bus" title="Bus">\n        bus\n       </a>\n       carrying evacuees crashed, killing four people, including three foreign tourists.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-uknews_26-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-uknews-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Coastal flooding caused by Wilma\'s storm surge and flooding from the outer bands was reported in many areas, particularly around\n       <a href="/wiki/Havana" title="Havana">\n        Havana\n       </a>\n       . More than 250 homes were heavily flooded and rescuers required\n       <a href="/wiki/Scuba_set" title="Scuba set">\n        scuba gear\n       </a>\n       , inflatable\n       <a href="/wiki/Raft" title="Raft">\n        rafts\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Amphibious_vehicle" title="Amphibious vehicle">\n        amphibious vehicles\n       </a>\n       to reach the most severely flooded areas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-petoskey_27-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-petoskey-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Havana was also without power and wind damage was reported as a result of winds up to 85\xc2\xa0mph (140\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-reuters-2006-24_28-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-reuters-2006-24-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Officials in Cuba estimated total damage to be about $700\xc2\xa0million.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReliefWeb-2006-24_4-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ReliefWeb-2006-24-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="United_States">\n        United States\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: United States">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Florida_2">\n        Florida\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Florida">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Wilma_in_Florida" title="Effects of Hurricane Wilma in Florida">\n        Effects of Hurricane Wilma in Florida\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Wilma_200510241245.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="720" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Hurricane_Wilma_200510241245.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Wilma_200510241245.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Hurricane_Wilma_200510241245.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Wilma_200510241245.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Hurricane_Wilma_200510241245.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Wilma_200510241245.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Wilma_200510241245.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The eye of Wilma over Florida, shortly after landfall\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       At least five hurricane-related deaths were reported in the United States, all in Florida, and there were at least 26 deaths indirectly related to Wilma.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">\n        <a href="#cite_note-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">\n        <a href="#cite_note-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Damage from Wilma was extensive and widespread over South Florida due to winds and flooding. After the hurricane had passed, a storm surge from the backwash of up to 8\xc2\xa0ft (2.4\xc2\xa0m) from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">\n        Gulf of Mexico\n       </a>\n       inundated a large portion of the lower Keys.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">\n        <a href="#cite_note-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The peak of the storm surge occurred when the eye of Wilma had already passed over the\n       <a href="/wiki/Naples,_Florida" title="Naples, Florida">\n        Naples\n       </a>\n       area, and the sustained winds during the surge were less than 40\xc2\xa0mph (64\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">\n        <a href="#cite_note-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Flood102405.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flood102405.JPG/220px-Flood102405.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flood102405.JPG/330px-Flood102405.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flood102405.JPG/440px-Flood102405.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Flood102405.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Storm surge from Wilma on\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Key_Haven" title="Key Haven">\n          Key Haven\n         </a>\n         , island suburb of Key West, Florida.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Hurricane Wilma caused widespread destruction of critical infrastructure, including power, water and sewer systems.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Florida_Power_and_Light" title="Florida Power and Light">\n        Florida Power and Light\n       </a>\n       , the largest electricity\n       <a href="/wiki/Utility" title="Utility">\n        utility\n       </a>\n       in the state, reported more than 3,241,000 customers had lost power,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">\n        <a href="#cite_note-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       equivalent to approximately 6,000,000\xc2\xa0people, with most residents getting power restored in 8\xe2\x80\x9315\xc2\xa0days. Running water was restored for most residents within 2\xc2\xa0days.\n       <a href="/wiki/Broward_County,_Florida" title="Broward County, Florida">\n        Broward\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Palm_Beach_County,_Florida" title="Palm Beach County, Florida">\n        Palm Beach\n       </a>\n       counties were hit particularly hard by the many tornadoes in the western portion of the hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_1-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Most notably in downtown\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fort_Lauderdale" title="Fort Lauderdale">\n        Fort Lauderdale\n       </a>\n       , there was significant damage to older buildings, including the Broward County Courthouse, School Board Building and taller area office buildings built before the implementation of stricter building codes after\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Andrew" title="Hurricane Andrew">\n        Hurricane Andrew\n       </a>\n       . The glass facades in a number of downtown buildings, notably the Templeton Building, were sheared off by high winds. Damage in Florida totaled $16.8 billion (2005\xc2\xa0USD).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">\n        <a href="#cite_note-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Elsewhere_in_the_United_States">\n        Elsewhere in the United States\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Elsewhere in the United States">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Few reports of effects from Hurricane Wilma exist in the United States outside of Florida, with minimal impact other than rain recorded in other states. Rainfall had extended into\n       <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(U.S._state)" title="Georgia (U.S. state)">\n        Georgia\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">\n        North Carolina\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/South_Carolina" title="South Carolina">\n        South Carolina\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">\n        Virginia\n       </a>\n       ; only a few areas had observed rain greater than two\xc2\xa0inches (51\xc2\xa0mm). Although only one\xe2\x80\x93two\xc2\xa0inches (25\xe2\x80\x9351\xc2\xa0mm) were reported in Georgia and South Carolina, Hurricane Wilma dropped approximately three\xc2\xa0inches (76\xc2\xa0mm) of rain on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Outer_Banks" title="Outer Banks">\n        Outer Banks\n       </a>\n       of North Carolina on October 25.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-hpcrain_35-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-hpcrain-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The remnants of Wilma combined with a nor\'easter, resulting in rainfall, snow, and strong winds across the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mid-Atlantic_states" title="Mid-Atlantic states">\n        Mid-Atlantic\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/New_England" title="New England">\n        New England\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Connecticut" title="Connecticut">\n        Connecticut\n       </a>\n       , strong winds felled tree limbs, trees, and electrical wires, resulting in scattered power outages in\n       <a href="/wiki/Ashford,_Connecticut" title="Ashford, Connecticut">\n        Ashford\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Pomfret,_Connecticut" title="Pomfret, Connecticut">\n        Pomfret\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Wethersfield,_Connecticut" title="Wethersfield, Connecticut">\n        Wethersfield\n       </a>\n       . Rainfall of 2 to 3 inches (51 to 76\xc2\xa0mm) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Litchfield_County,_Connecticut" title="Litchfield County, Connecticut">\n        Litchfield County\n       </a>\n       caused the\n       <a href="/wiki/Housatonic_River" title="Housatonic River">\n        Housatonic River\n       </a>\n       to reach a crest of 7.18\xc2\xa0ft (2.19\xc2\xa0m) at\n       <a href="/wiki/Falls_Village,_Connecticut" title="Falls Village, Connecticut">\n        Falls Village\n       </a>\n       late on October\xc2\xa026. Minor flooding was reported in the county. Strong winds in\n       <a href="/wiki/Rhode_Island" title="Rhode Island">\n        Rhode Island\n       </a>\n       knocked down a large tree onto\n       <a href="/wiki/Interstate_95" title="Interstate 95">\n        Interstate 95\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Providence,_Rhode_Island" title="Providence, Rhode Island">\n        Providence\n       </a>\n       , blocking a few northbound lanes. Additionally, several trees, power lines, and tree limbs were downed in\n       <a href="/wiki/Exeter,_Rhode_Island" title="Exeter, Rhode Island">\n        Exeter\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Tiverton,_Rhode_Island" title="Tiverton, Rhode Island">\n        Tiverton\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/West_Greenwich,_Rhode_Island" title="West Greenwich, Rhode Island">\n        West Greenwich\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Woonsocket,_Rhode_Island" title="Woonsocket, Rhode Island">\n        Woonsocket\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stormdata_36-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stormdata-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts" title="Massachusetts">\n        Massachusetts\n       </a>\n       , there was between 2 and 2.5\xc2\xa0in (51 and 64\xc2\xa0mm) of rain, damaging winds, and coastal flooding in the eastern half of the state. Wind gusts between 44 and 47\xc2\xa0mph (71 and 76\xc2\xa0km/h) were common, with a gust as strong as 66\xc2\xa0mph (106\xc2\xa0km/h) was recorded at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Blue_Hill_Meteorological_Observatory" title="Blue Hill Meteorological Observatory">\n        Blue Hill Meteorological Observatory\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Milton,_Massachusetts" title="Milton, Massachusetts">\n        Milton\n       </a>\n       . The strong winds downed limbs, trees, and wires, resulting in thousands of people without power. In addition, a trailer was blown over on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Bourne_Bridge" title="Bourne Bridge">\n        Bourne Bridge\n       </a>\n       .
