A tree struck a car in\n       <a href="/wiki/Fall_River,_Massachusetts" title="Fall River, Massachusetts">\n        Fall River\n       </a>\n       , while trees fell on houses in\n       <a href="/wiki/Boxford,_Massachusetts" title="Boxford, Massachusetts">\n        Boxford\n       </a>\n       and in\n       <a href="/wiki/Peabody,_Massachusetts" title="Peabody, Massachusetts">\n        Peabody\n       </a>\n       . In Bridgewater, several power poles and trees were toppled. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Green_Line_(MBTA)" title="Green Line (MBTA)">\n        Green Line\n       </a>\n       trains were blocked in\n       <a href="/wiki/Newton,_Massachusetts" title="Newton, Massachusetts">\n        Newton\n       </a>\n       after a tree fell at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Riverside_(MBTA_station)" title="Riverside (MBTA station)">\n        Riverside Station\n       </a>\n       . The towns of\n       <a href="/wiki/Hull,_Massachusetts" title="Hull, Massachusetts">\n        Hull\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Marblehead,_Massachusetts" title="Marblehead, Massachusetts">\n        Marblehead\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Marshfield,_Massachusetts" title="Marshfield, Massachusetts">\n        Marshfield\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Nantucket,_Massachusetts" title="Nantucket, Massachusetts">\n        Nantucket\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Salem,_Massachusetts" title="Salem, Massachusetts">\n        Salem\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Scituate,_Massachusetts" title="Scituate, Massachusetts">\n        Scituate\n       </a>\n       experienced coastal flooding. Several boats broke from their moorings and washed ashore.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stormdata_36-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stormdata-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The remnants of Wilma and the nor\'easter brought snowfall to southern\n       <a href="/wiki/Vermont" title="Vermont">\n        Vermont\n       </a>\n       from October\xc2\xa025 to October\xc2\xa026. Up to 20\xc2\xa0in (510\xc2\xa0mm) of snow was accumulated at higher elevations. In\n       <a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">\n        Maine\n       </a>\n       , wind gusts between 55 and 65\xc2\xa0mph (89 and 105\xc2\xa0km/h) occurred near the coast, particularly in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Down_East" title="Down East">\n        Down East\n       </a>\n       region. The combination of strong winds and saturated ground from prior heavy rainfall over a period of several weeks caused trees and many branches to topple. These falling trees and limbs downed many power lines, resulting in numerous electrical outages. Farther inland, the two systems left 3 to 8\xc2\xa0in (76 to 203\xc2\xa0mm) of snow in many areas and localized totals of 12 to 16\xc2\xa0in (300 to 410\xc2\xa0mm) across higher terrain. The snow brought down trees and power lines, leaving about 25,000 customers lost power for varying amounts of time during the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stormdata_36-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stormdata-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Bahamas">\n        Bahamas\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Bahamas">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Wilma_in_The_Bahamas" title="Effects of Hurricane Wilma in The Bahamas">\n        Effects of Hurricane Wilma in The Bahamas\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       While passing the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bahamas" title="Bahamas">\n        Bahamas\n       </a>\n       , the hurricane produced hurricane-force winds\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jm_37-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-jm-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and a powerful\n       <a href="/wiki/Storm_surge" title="Storm surge">\n        storm surge\n       </a>\n       , flooding southwestern coastal areas of Grand Bahama and destroying hundreds of buildings. In western settlements on the island of Grand Bahama, graves were washed up with skeletal remains lying in the streets. Damage totaled about $100\xc2\xa0million (2005\xc2\xa0USD, $105\xc2\xa0million 2007\xc2\xa0USD), almost entirely on the western half of the island. The central portion of Grand Bahama, including in and around\n       <a href="/wiki/Freeport,_Bahamas" title="Freeport, Bahamas">\n        Freeport\n       </a>\n       , reported minor to moderate damage, while the eastern end received little to no damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pbp124_38-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-pbp124-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One child died on the island from the flooding. Elsewhere in the Bahamas, moderate damage occurred on\n       <a href="/wiki/Bimini" title="Bimini">\n        Bimini\n       </a>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ifrc1_14-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ifrc1-14">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Abaco_Islands" title="Abaco Islands">\n        Abaco\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pbp111_39-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-pbp111-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       while islands farther to the south reported minimal wind damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ifrc1_14-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ifrc1-14">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Wilma struck the Bahamas during the filming of Disney\'s\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Pirates_of_the_Caribbean:_Dead_Man%27s_Chest" title="Pirates of the Caribbean: Dead Man\'s Chest">\n         Pirates of the Caribbean: Dead Man\'s Chest\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       . The service roads were destroyed and several trailers turned over. The two principal ships, the\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Black_Pearl" title="Black Pearl">\n         Black Pearl\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       and\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Flying_Dutchman_(Pirates_of_the_Caribbean)" title="Flying Dutchman (Pirates of the Caribbean)">\n         The Flying Dutchman\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , were relatively undamaged and the cast and crew were evacuated on the Friday before the hurricane hit.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40">\n        <a href="#cite_note-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Aftermath">\n        Aftermath\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Aftermath">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:FEMA_-_18119_-_Photograph_by_Jocelyn_Augustino_taken_on_10-29-2005_in_Florida.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/FEMA_-_18119_-_Photograph_by_Jocelyn_Augustino_taken_on_10-29-2005_in_Florida.jpg/220px-FEMA_-_18119_-_Photograph_by_Jocelyn_Augustino_taken_on_10-29-2005_in_Florida.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/FEMA_-_18119_-_Photograph_by_Jocelyn_Augustino_taken_on_10-29-2005_in_Florida.jpg/330px-FEMA_-_18119_-_Photograph_by_Jocelyn_Augustino_taken_on_10-29-2005_in_Florida.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/FEMA_-_18119_-_Photograph_by_Jocelyn_Augustino_taken_on_10-29-2005_in_Florida.jpg/440px-FEMA_-_18119_-_Photograph_by_Jocelyn_Augustino_taken_on_10-29-2005_in_Florida.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:FEMA_-_18119_-_Photograph_by_Jocelyn_Augustino_taken_on_10-29-2005_in_Florida.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Federal_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Federal Emergency Management Agency">\n          Federal Emergency Management Agency\n         </a>\n         (FEMA) Disaster Medical Assistance Team checks a patient outside of the JFK Medical Center (\n         <a href="/wiki/Boynton_Beach,_Florida" title="Boynton Beach, Florida">\n          Boynton Beach\n         </a>\n         ). The DMAT is set up in the entry way of the hospital to assist in seeing the increase flow of patients due to Hurricane Wilma.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="United_States_2">\n        United States\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: United States">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Florida\'s sugar industry was greatly affected; the cropping had already started and had to be halted indefinitely. Damage to sugarcane crops was critical and widespread.\n       <a href="/wiki/Citrus_canker" title="Citrus canker">\n        Citrus canker\n       </a>\n       spread rapidly throughout southern Florida following Hurricane Wilma, creating further hardships on an already stressed citrus economy due to damage from Wilma and previous years\' hurricanes. Citrus production estimates fell to a low of 158\xc2\xa0million boxes for the 2005\xe2\x80\x932006 production seasons from a high of 240\xc2\xa0million for 2003\xe2\x80\x932004.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fl_citrus_41-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fl_citrus-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In January 2006, artists were invited to exhibit sculptures inspired by the storm in an outdoor exhibit at\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fort_Zachary_Taylor" title="Fort Zachary Taylor">\n        Fort Zachary Taylor\n       </a>\n       near the new NWS hurricane and weather forecasting center in Key West, Florida.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       By late-September 2010, roughly $9.2\xc2\xa0billion had been paid for more than 1\xc2\xa0million insurance claims that had been filed throughout Florida in relation to Hurricane Wilma.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n        <a href="#cite_note-42">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mexico_3">\n        Mexico\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Mexico">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The popular Mexican resort towns of\n       <a href="/wiki/Playa_del_Carmen" title="Playa del Carmen">\n        Playa del Carmen\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Cozumel" title="Cozumel">\n        Cozumel\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Canc%C3%BAn" title="Canc\xc3\xban">\n        Canc\xc3\xban\n       </a>\n       all suffered significant damage from Wilma, causing a major loss of tourism income. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Los_Premios_MTV_Latinoam%C3%A9rica" title="Los Premios MTV Latinoam\xc3\xa9rica">\n        MTV Video Music Awards Latin America\n       </a>\n       2005 was to be held Wednesday, October 19 at the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Xcaret_Eco_Park" title="Xcaret Eco Park">\n        Xcaret Eco Park\n       </a>\n       (close to Playa del Carmen) in Quintana Roo, Mexico. The 2005 edition of these awards was postponed, however, because of the approach of Hurricane Wilma toward the Mexican Riviera Maya. MTV had moved the date from October 20 to 19 in an attempt to avoid the hurricane, but eventually decided to cancel the show. The 2005 edition eventually took place using a modified format on December 22.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Cuba_3">\n        Cuba\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Cuba">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The United States offered emergency aid to\n       <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">\n        Cuba\n       </a>\n       , and to the surprise of the State Department, the Cuban government accepted. Many times in the past, including during\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Dennis" title="Hurricane Dennis">\n        Hurricane Dennis\n       </a>\n       , the United States offered aid, but the Cuban government declined. The State Department sent three damage assessors to\n       <a href="/wiki/Havana" title="Havana">\n        Havana\n       </a>\n       to determine their needs.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">\n        <a href="#cite_note-43">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Retirement">\n        Retirement\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Retirement">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Atlantic_hurricane_names" title="List of retired Atlantic hurricane names">\n        List of retired Atlantic hurricane names\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Due to significant damage in Mexico and Florida, the name Wilma was officially retired in April 2006 by the\n       <a href="/wiki/World_Meteorological_Organization" title="World Meteorological Organization">\n        World Meteorological Organization\n       </a>\n       , and will never be used for an\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/North_Atlantic_tropical_cyclone" title="North Atlantic tropical cyclone">\n        Atlantic storm\n       </a>\n       again. It was replaced by Whitney in\n       <a href="/wiki/2011_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2011 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2011\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">\n        <a href="#cite_note-44">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Records_and_naming">\n        Records and naming\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Records and naming">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <table align="right" border="1" class="wikitable" style="font-size: 92%;">\n       <tr>\n        <th colspan="6" style="background:#ccf;">\n         <a href="/wiki/List_of_the_most_intense_tropical_cyclones#Atlantic_Ocean" title="List of the most intense tropical cyclones">\n          Most intense Atlantic hurricanes\n         </a>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th rowspan="2">\n         Rank\n        </th>\n        <th rowspan="2">\n         Hurricane\n        </th>\n        <th rowspan="2">\n         Season\n        </th>\n        <th colspan="2">\n         Pressure\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         hPa\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         inHg\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         1\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-selflink selflink">\n          Wilma\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a 26.05\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         2\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Gilbert" title="Hurricane Gilbert">\n          Gilbert\n   888\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.23\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         3\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1935_Labor_Day_hurricane" title="1935 Labor Day hurricane">\n          "Labor Day"\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1935_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1935 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          1935\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         892\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.34\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         4\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Rita" title="Hurricane Rita">\n          Rita\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2005\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         895\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.43\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         5\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Allen" title="Hurricane Allen">\n          Allen\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1980_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1980 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          1980\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         899\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.55\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         6\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Camille" title="Hurricane Camille">\n          Camille\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1969_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1969 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          1969\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         900\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.58\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         7\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katrina" title="Hurricane Katrina">\n          Katrina\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2005\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         902\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.64\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th rowspan="2">\n         8\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Mitch" title="Hurricane Mitch">\n          Mitch\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1998_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1998 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          1998\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         905\n        </td>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         26.73\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Dean" title="Hurricane Dean">\n          Dean\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2007 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2007\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         10\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Maria" title="Hurricane Maria">\n          Maria\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2017 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2017\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         908\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         26.81\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr class="small">\n        <th colspan="6">\n         Source: HURDAT\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HURDAT_45-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-HURDAT-45">\n           [45]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The storm was named "Wilma," the first time the \'W\' name was used in the Atlantic Basin since alphabetical naming began in 1950. With Wilma, the 2005 hurricane season broke the record for most storms in a season previously held by the\n       <a href="/wiki/1933_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1933 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        1933 season\n       </a>\n       . Moving slowly over warm water with little\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       , Wilma strengthened steadily and became a hurricane on October 18. The thirteenth hurricane of the season, Wilma broke the record set in\n       <a href="/wiki/1969_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1969 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        1969\n       </a>\n       for most storms of hurricane strength in one season for the Atlantic Basin.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Barometric_pressure" title="Barometric pressure">\n        barometric pressure\n       </a>\n       measured in Wilma, 882\xc2\xa0mbar (26.05\xc2\xa0inHg), is currently the lowest recorded pressure for a tropical cyclone in the Atlantic Basin, as well as the second-lowest pressure for any cyclone measured in the Western Hemisphere, only after\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Patricia" title="Hurricane Patricia">\n        Hurricane Patricia\n       </a>\n       ten years later in the Eastern Pacific. It also reached its 882\xc2\xa0mbar (26.05\xc2\xa0inHg) pressure in a span of 24\xc2\xa0hours, making it the fastest pressure drop of any storm in the Atlantic Basin, although\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Felix" title="Hurricane Felix">\n        Hurricane Felix\n       </a>\n       of 2007 reached a greater windspeed rise in 51\xc2\xa0hours. At its peak intensity, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">\n        eye\n       </a>\n       of Wilma was about 2.3 miles (3.7\xc2\xa0km) in diameter, the smallest known eye of a tropical cyclone.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_1-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In Mexico,\n       <a href="/wiki/Isla_Mujeres" title="Isla Mujeres">\n        Isla Mujeres\n       </a>\n       reported 64\xc2\xa0inches (1,625.6\xc2\xa0mm) of rainfall\xe2\x80\x94five times what\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Gilbert" title="Hurricane Gilbert">\n        Hurricane Gilbert\n       </a>\n       dropped. This set a 24-hour rainfall record for the country of Mexico, and was the highest point total for rainfall from a tropical cyclone since\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Mitch" title="Hurricane Mitch">\n        Hurricane Mitch\n       </a>\n       in 1998. Wilma is also the costliest hurricane in Mexican history.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Wilma was the first retired "W" name since the World Meteorological Organization started retiring names in 1954, it was the strongest Atlantic hurricane to be retired, and when it was retired, it made 2005 the season with the most retired names, with five; the old record was a three-way tie with four names retired in 1955, 1995, and 2004. Wilma was replaced with the name Whitney. Had the unnamed\n       <a href="/wiki/2005_Azores_subtropical_storm" title="2005 Azores subtropical storm">\n        2005 Azores subtropical storm\n       </a>\n       been operationally recognized it would have been named Subtropical Storm Tammy, and storms forming after October\xc2\xa04 would have been moved one name down the list. Wilma would have consequently been given the name\n       <i>\n        Alpha\n       </i>\n       , in accordance with the convention to name tropical cyclones after the Greek alphabet if the scheduled list of names runs out.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">\n        <a href="#cite_note-46">\n         [46]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AOML_FAQ_47-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-AOML_FAQ-47">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n        See also\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Wilma&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: See also">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div aria-label="Portals" class="noprint portal plainlist tright" role="navigation" style="margin:0.5em 0 0.5em 1em;border:solid #aaa 1px">\n       <ul style="display:table;box-sizing:border-box;padding:0.1em;max-width:175px;background:#f9f9f9;font-size:85%;line-height:110%;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold">\n        <li style="display:table-row">\n         <span style="display:table-cell;padding:0.2em;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center">\n          <img alt="" class="noviewer" data-file-height="2004" data-file-width="3032" height="21" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Cyclone_Catarina_from_the_ISS_on_March_26_2004.JPG/32px-Cyclone_Catarina_from_the_ISS_on_March_26_2004.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Cyclone_Catarina_from_the_ISS_on_March_26_2004.JPG/48px-Cyclone_Catarina_from_the_ISS_on_March_26_2004.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Cyclone_Catarina_from_the_ISS_on_March_26_2004.JPG/64px-Cyclone_Catarina_from_the_ISS_on_March_26_2004.JPG 2x" width="32"/>\n         </span>\n         <span style="display:table-cell;padding:0.2em 0.2em 0.2em 0.3em;vertical-align:middle">\n          <a href="/wiki/Portal:Tropical_cyclones" title="Portal:Tropical cyclones">\n           Tropical cyclones portal\n          </a>\n         </span>\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </div>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season_storms" title="List of 2005 Atlantic hurricane season storms">\n         List of 2005 Atlantic hurricane season storms\n        </a>\n       </li>\n
